\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$，最“分/解析”的特征分解方法是 \textcolor{Maroon}{Jordan-Chevalley 分解}及其等价方法。--- 然而，由于 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\bar{k}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\symup{z}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 是个 2D 分布的矩阵场，只能对其进行批量 \textcolor{Maroon}{Jordan-Chevalley 分解}，而这只能是数值的，并且在例外点（EP）附近在理论和数值上均是不稳定的\cite{molerNineteenDubiousWays2003}。{\four} 所有病态的 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\bar{k}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\symup{z}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$，如果没有通过 \textcolor{Maroon}{Jordan-Chevalley 分解}或其等价的方法，获得其广义（子）本征系统，那么在其非子基矢空间中，总存在接近简并的特征向量，且无法再被进一步区分，不论是解析地还是数值地。此时，\textcolor{Maroon}{矩阵指数解}在形式和内容上将不存在任何优势，相比接下来提出的方法。

作为通过特征分解，计算并区分近简并特征向量、正反向本征波，方便计算\textcolor{Maroon}{矩阵指数}，并有可能避免\textcolor{Maroon}{矩阵指数}发散的强大理论工具，对矩阵场 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\bar{k}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\symup{z}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 执行批量 \textcolor{Maroon}{Jordan-Chevalley 分解}在数值上的不稳定性，迫使我们寻找矩阵形式的试探本征解 \bref{eq:vec-matrix_exp} 和与之适配的 \textcolor{Maroon}{Jordan-Chevalley 分解}技术的组合的下位替代。

\clearpage
\vspace*{-8.0em}

\marginLeft[-2.4em]{ssec:E-waveq-linear}\subsection{线性均匀非局域、非矩阵指数 $\bar{E}$ 波动方程}\label{ssec:E-waveq-linear}

既然\textcolor{Maroon}{矩阵指数}形式的试探解 \bref{eq:vec-matrix_exp} 除了能区分光学奇点 or 例外点附近，接近简并的特征向量外，无法带来更多的好处，该节则尝试放弃该形式，转而采取更常见的\textcolor{Maroon}{线性叠加的单色平面波基}形式的试探解
\begin{subequations} \label{eq:plane_wave_basis}
\begin{align}
	\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{\bar{E}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} &:= \leftindex_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \;\! \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{\bar{E}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} = \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} ~, \label{eq:vec-plane_wave_basis} \\
	\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{E}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} &:= \leftindex_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \;\! \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{E}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} = \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{g}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} ~, \label{eq:components-plane_wave_basis}
\end{align}
\end{subequations}
当 \bref{eq:k_check_j^nabla} 即算子 $\mathcolor{gray}{k^\nabla_{\check{1}}}$ 中的 $\mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z}$ 作用于 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify5} 的试探解 \bref{eq:components-plane_wave_basis} 的\textcolor{Maroon}{每个（第$\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}$个）模式}即 $
\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{E}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} = \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{g}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$ 之后，结果从 \bref{eq:matrix_exp-dz,eq:matrix_exp-ddz} 降阶为
\begin{subequations}
\begin{align}
	\mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z} \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{E}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} = \mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z} \left( \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{g}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \right) = \left( \mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} + \mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z} \right) \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{g}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} ~, \label{eq:plane_wave_basis-dz} \\
	\mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z^2} \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{E}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} = \left( - \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}^{\;\! \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath} 2} + 2 \mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z} + \mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z^2} \right) \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{g}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} ~, \label{eq:plane_wave_basis-ddz}
\end{align}
\end{subequations}
使用 \bref{eq:plane_wave_basis-dz,eq:plane_wave_basis-ddz}，将 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify5-vector} 的左侧分离出线性、非线性算子 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{\bar{\bar{L}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}, \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{21}{\bar{\bar{V}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$
\begin{subequations}
	\abovedisplayskip=-5pt
\begin{align}
	\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{32}{\bar{\bar{L}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{295}{\bar{E}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} &:= \left( \bar{\bar{\varepsilon}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} + \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} \mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} - \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1} \check{2}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{2}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \right) \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{295}{\bar{E}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} ~, \label{eq:plane_wave_basis_eq-left_linear_operator} \\
	\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{\bar{\bar{V}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} &:= \left[ \left( \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\symup{z}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} + \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1} \symup{z}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} 2 \mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \right) \mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z} + \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\symup{z} \symup{z}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} \mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z^2} \right] \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} ~, \label{eq:plane_wave_basis_eq-left_nonlinear_operator}
\end{align}
\end{subequations}
其中，类似 \bref{eq:barbar_k_check_j} 地定义了
\begin{align} \label{eq:k_check_j}
	\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{\symup{\jmath}}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} := \mathcolor{gray}{k_{\symup{x}}} ~\textcolor{Maroon}{\text{或}}~ \mathcolor{gray}{k_{\symup{y}}} ~\textcolor{Maroon}{\text{或}}~ \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}~,
\end{align}
有了 $\left( \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}, \mathcolor{gray}{\bar{k}_{\symup{\rho}}} \right)$ 域中，通过 \bref{eq:plane_wave_basis_eq-left_linear_operator} 定义的线性算子 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{\bar{\bar{L}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 和 \bref{eq:plane_wave_basis_eq-left_nonlinear_operator} 定义的非线性算子 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{21}{\bar{\bar{V}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 后，\bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify5-vector} 可进一步简写作 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6}。

如 \bref{ssec:Exp-waveq} 所言，假设 \bref{eq:L+V-decompose,eq:L+V-decompose2} 中任意一个成立，则 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6} 可以进一步拆分为 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-L,eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V}；再代入 \bref{eq:plane_wave_basis_eq-left_linear_operator,eq:plane_wave_basis_eq-left_nonlinear_operator}，最终得 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-L3,eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V2} 的降阶版：
\begin{subequations}
\begin{align}
	\det \left[ \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{32}{\bar{\bar{L}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \right] &= \det \left[ \bar{\bar{\varepsilon}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} + \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} \mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}} - \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1} \check{2}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{2}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}} \right] = 0 ~, \label{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-L3'} \\
	\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{\bar{\bar{V}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}
	&= \left[ \left( \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\symup{z}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} + \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1} \symup{z}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} 2 \mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\check{1}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}} \right) \mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z} + \bar{\bar{\zeta}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \mathcolor{gray}{\symup{z} \symup{z}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{(1)}} \mathcolor{gray}{\nabla_z^2} \right] \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \label{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V2'} \\
	&= - \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{23}{\bar{\bar{\bar{\chi}}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\imath \jmath l}}_{\mathcolor{gray}{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{(2)}} ~{}^{\mathcolor{gray}{*}}_{\mathcolor{gray}{*}} \left[ \left( \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \right) ~\mathcolor{gray}{\widetilde \circledast}~ \left( \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{l}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{l}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \right) \right] \label{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V3'} ~.
\end{align}
\end{subequations}
尽管从 \bref{eq:barbar_k_check_j} 中的矩阵 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\bar{k}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\symup{z}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 到 \bref{eq:k_check_j} 中的标量 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$，波动/特征方程的“自变量”阶数下降了，但代价是它包含了每个模式 $\textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}$（线性晶体光学），甚至模式的组合 $\textcolor{Maroon}{\imath},\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath},\textcolor{Maroon}{l}$（非线性晶体光学）。

\bref{ssec:E-waveq-linear} 表明，当试探解的形式，从\textcolor{Maroon}{矩阵指数} \bref{eq:vec-matrix_exp} 简化为 \textcolor{Maroon}{线性叠加的单色平面波基} 后，线性无源齐次和非线性有源非齐次波动方程，分别从 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-L3,eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V2} 过渡到 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-L3',eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V2'}，使两个方程的解更容易获得。

以线性晶体光学为例，\bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-L3'} 只是一个关于标量场 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$ 的\textcolor{Maroon}{六次方程}，可以使用 \textcolor{Maroon}{QR 分解}、\textcolor{Maroon}{Schur 分解}、求根公式\Footnote{原则上，5 次方程及以上没有求根公式，但特定系数和结构下可能存在因式分解的办法和根式解。}、牛顿迭代法，获得全部 6 个本征值 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$（即 \bref{eq:kz-non_diagonalization} 中的 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{22}{\lambda}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$）\cite{raabMultipoleTheoryElectromagnetism2004}。将这 6 个本征值分别代入 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{\bar{\bar{L}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 的零空间\cite{changWavePropagationBianisotropic2014,chernChiralSurfaceWaves2017}，可以分别获得与之对应的 6 个本征向量/偏振态 $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$（即 \bref{eq:kz-non_diagonalization} 中的 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{v}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$），并通过对比 $\textcolor{Maroon}{\text{Re}} \left[ \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{S}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\mathrm{z}} \right]$\Footnote{$\textcolor{Maroon}{\text{Re}} \left[ \cdot \right]$ 代表对 $\cdot$ 取实部。\textcolor{Maroon}{Poynting 矢量}一般采取 \textcolor{Maroon}{Abraham 形式}，即 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{\bar{S}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} := \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{\bar{E}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} \times \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{23}{\bar{H}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$，这使得对能流密度矢量场 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{\bar{S}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$、能量密度标量场 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{05}{W}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$\cite{chen-zhuChenZhuxieUndergraduate_courses2024} 均需要评估原点平移不变性，正如反射场景一样\cite{raabMultipoleTheoryElectromagnetism2004}(\textcolor{Maroon}{p 206})；尽管波动方程本身是原点无关的（透射场景），但除此以外所有独立涉及本构关系的部分都需要评估。} 与 $0$ 的大小，将其分类为 3 个正向、3 个反向传播的本征波\cite{asoubarSimulationBirefringenceEffects2015,zhangFullyVectorialSimulation2016,liReformulationFourierModal1998}。其中，总有 2 个正向、2 个反向传播的横模，剩下 1 个正向、1 个反向传播的纵模，这种电场偏振方向接近平行于波矢传播方向的纵波，是“附加波”的一个例子，是高阶多极子带来的空间色散的结果\cite{raabMultipoleTheoryElectromagnetism2004}(\textcolor{Maroon}{p 116})。

由于试探解的核心从 \bref{ssec:Exp-solution-linear} 中的 \bref{eq:barbar_k_check_j} 过渡到了 \bref{ssec:E-waveq-linear} 中的 \bref{eq:k_check_j}，这使得“波矢”从 2 阶 3 维张量（场）$\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\bar{k}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\symup{z}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 降阶至标量（场）$\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$，收缩的解空间将所有子特征向量 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\nu}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}}$ 排挤出去，作为“父特征向量” $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{v}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} = \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$ 放进 $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$ 中，并因此一旦简并则无法再被分辨；剩下的特征值仍保留在 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\bar{k}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\symup{z}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 的 \textcolor{Maroon}{标准型} $\overline{\overline{\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}}}$ 的对角线元素 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 中。然而，若 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\bar{k}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\symup{z}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 是非厄米的且非正规的\cite{wiersigDistanceExceptionalPoints2022}，标量特征值 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 与父特征向量 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{v}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} = \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$ 的组合，便再也无法比肩于 \bref{eq:kz-Jordan_decompose} 中 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\bar{k}}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\symup{z}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 的 \textcolor{Maroon}{Jordan 标准型} $\bar{\bar{J}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}} = \overline{\overline{\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}}} + \bar{\bar{M}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 和相应的子特征向量 $\Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{\bar{\nu}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{\imath}}$ 的组合了。

在 \bref{eq:weak_modulated_linear_sus} 和 \bref{eq:L+V-decompose}（或\bref{eq:L+V-decompose2}）的条件下，进一步假设：
\begin{align} \label{eq:L+V-polar}
	\textcolor{Maroon}{\text{在 2D 傅立叶空间中，线性、非线性晶体光学本征模均不含} ~\mathcolor{gray}{z} }~,
\end{align}
即文献\cite{xieAnalytic3DVector}中的 Eq. (S55b)。该假设在 \bref{eq:weak_modulated_linear_sus} 条件下的线性晶体光学中基本成立，但它在非线性晶体光学中是否成立，还须进一步探讨。在此条件下，\textcolor{Maroon}{线性叠加的单色平面波基} \bref{eq:plane_wave_basis} 的\textcolor{Maroon}{非相位部分} $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$ 总可以因式分解为“\textcolor{Maroon}{复振幅} $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$· \textcolor{Maroon}{偏振态} $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{08}{\bar{\mathsfit{g}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$”之积（\textcolor{Maroon}{矩阵指数}形式的 \bref{eq:vec-matrix_exp} 也可以，但没必要分解）：
\begin{subequations} \label{eq:polar_amp}
\begin{align}
	\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{10}{\bar{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} &:= \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{08}{\bar{\mathsfit{g}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} ~, \label{eq:vec-polar_amp} \\
	\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{08}{g}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} &:= \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathsfit{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1}} ~, \label{eq:components-polar_amp}
\end{align}
\end{subequations}
即三分量之间的比例，完全由不含 $\mathcolor{gray}{z}$ 的\textcolor{Maroon}{偏振态} $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{08}{\bar{\mathsfit{g}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$ 独立控制（与\textcolor{Maroon}{复振幅} $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$ 无关），而三分量的幅值却共享同一个含 $\mathcolor{gray}{z}$ 的增幅因子，即按\textcolor{Maroon}{复振幅} $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$ 的比例同步缩放。注意，这里分别给\textcolor{Maroon}{偏振态} 和 \textcolor{Maroon}{复振幅} 赋予了单独的字体 $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{08}{\bar{\mathsfit{g}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$（\textbackslash mathsfit）和 $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$（\textbackslash mathtt），见 \bref{hook:mathsfit,hook:mathtt}。

从自由度上看，\bref{eq:polar_amp} 左侧，在 $\mathcolor{gray}{z}$ 上的自由度等于矢量的分量个数，即维度 3；而该方程的右侧，在 $\mathcolor{gray}{z}$ 上的自由度，为 \textcolor{Maroon}{偏振态} $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{08}{\bar{\mathsfit{g}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$ 的自由度 $+$ \textcolor{Maroon}{复振幅} $\Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$ 的自由度 $= 2 + 1 = 3$。因此，从这个角度，该分解并没有降低表示自由度，所以是可接受的。在 \bref{eq:polar_amp} 的分解表示下，\bref{eq:plane_wave_basis} 进一步细化为
\begin{subequations} \label{eq:polar_amp_phase}
\begin{align}
	\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{\bar{E}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} &:= \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{08}{\bar{\mathsfit{g}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} ~, \label{eq:vec-polar_amp_phase} \\
	\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{E}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} &:= \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{02}{\mathtt{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \Xint{{}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}}{08}{\mathsfit{g}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \hat{1}} \mathbb{e}^{\mathbb{i} \Xint{\begin{smallmatrix} ~ \\ {}^{}_{\mathcolor{gray}{-}} \\ ~ \end{smallmatrix}}{15}{k}_{\symup{z}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}} \mathcolor{gray}{z}} ~, \label{eq:components-polar_amp_phase}
\end{align}
\end{subequations}
注，在傅立叶空间中，电场 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{\bar{E}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$ 以外的电磁场量 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{\bar{D}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}, \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{25}{\bar{B}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}, \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{22}{\bar{H}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$，（在形式上）都可以按 \bref{eq:matrix_exp,eq:plane_wave_basis} 进行基分解（为对应的\textcolor{Maroon}{非相位}·\textcolor{Maroon}{相位}两部分之积），并按 \bref{eq:polar_amp_phase} 分解为\textcolor{Maroon}{复振幅}·\textcolor{Maroon}{偏振态}·\textcolor{Maroon}{相位}三部分之积， --- 通过将它们的\textcolor{Maroon}{非相位}部分 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{07}{\bar{d}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}, \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{09}{\bar{b}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}, \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{10}{\bar{h}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}}$ 分解为\textcolor{Maroon}{复振幅}·\textcolor{Maroon}{偏振态}两部分之积 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{07}{\bar{d}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} = \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{02}{\mathtt{d}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{06}{\bar{\mathsfit{d}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}, \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{09}{\bar{b}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} = \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{02}{\mathtt{b}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{06}{\bar{\mathsfit{b}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}, \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{10}{\bar{h}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} = \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{02}{\mathtt{h}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}_{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{z}} \Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{06}{\bar{\mathsfit{h}}}^{\;\!\mathcolor{gray}{\omega} \textcolor{Maroon}{\jmath}}$，像 \bref{eq:polar_amp} 一样。

从 \bref{eq:polar_amp} 中可以清晰地看出，

将 6 个偏振态 ，区分出来的 3 个正向传播的模式，进一步

可以看到，相比 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-L4,eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V2}， \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-L3',eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V2'} 更容易求解。然而，随之而来的代价便是（仍以线性晶体光学所涉及的 $\Xint{\mathcolor{gray}{-}}{30}{\bar{\bar{L}}}^{\;\! \mathcolor{gray}{\omega}}$ 为例），由于本征值-本征向量的一一对应关系，当本征值简并时，本征向量要么可以是任意的非平行基（对应恶魔点），要么也是简并的（对应例外点/奇点），--- 以至于在恶魔点（DPs）处和例外点（EPs）附近，需要对特征向量手动添加额外的特殊处理，甚至即使施行了“外科手术”，也无济于事：特别是在例外点附近。此时，在例外点附近的电磁场传播的动力学演化过程，将无法通过\textcolor{Maroon}{线性叠加的单色平面波基}\bref{eq:plane_wave_basis}及其配套的方法计算，而被“禁止察看”。

然而，对于线性晶体光学而言，在空间频率域 $\mathcolor{gray}{\bar{k}_{\symup{\rho}}} \in \mathcolor{gray}{\bar{\mathbb{R}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{2}}}$ 内，由于例外点本身通常只以有限个点（一般最多 8 个\cite{berryOpticalSingularitiesBirefringent2003,berryOpticalSingularitiesBianisotropic2005,sturmPropagationElectromagneticWaves,sturmSingularOpticalAxes2016a,grundmannOpticallyAnisotropicMedia2017}）存在，少数情况下才以线、面的形式覆盖不可计算区域\cite{xieAnalytic3DVector}，--- 因此，大多数情况下，空间频率域 $\mathcolor{gray}{\bar{k}_{\symup{\rho}}} \in \mathcolor{gray}{\bar{\mathbb{R}}_{\textcolor{Maroon}{2}}}$ 内剩余的大面积无光学奇点的广袤空旷区域是可计算的，以至于减轻了采取\textcolor{Maroon}{线性叠加的单色平面波基}形式的试探解 \bref{eq:plane_wave_basis} 的问题的严重性。除此之外，该基没有其他劣势，且除此之外全是优势（如方便计算、遵循传统、比较物理、易于理解）。在对比并评估完成 \bref{ssec:Exp-solution-linear,ssec:E-waveq-linear} 中的两种基各自的利弊后，本文后续选择 \bref{eq:plane_wave_basis} 而不是 \bref{eq:matrix_exp} 作为本征模/波/基/态（的形式），并因此保持光学奇点内部的不可探测性（这一点比较像黑洞），即简并本征向量的不可区分性。

\marginLeft[-2.4em]{ssec:E-waveq-nonlinear}\subsection{非线性非均匀局域单色平面波 $\bar{E}$ 波动方程}\label{ssec:E-waveq-nonlinear}

上面两小节，即\bref{ssec:Exp-solution-linear,ssec:E-waveq-linear}，从线性晶体光学的角度，对比并确定/选用了傅立叶基/分量的形式为 \bref{eq:plane_wave_basis}。现在这一节将转而预处理非线性晶体光学的第一性原理 \bref{eq:nonlinear(2)-wave_wkrho-simplify6-V2'}。
